						amount > 24
					}

						amount < 79
					}
				}

					amount = -5

			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						controller = {
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					has_resources_amount = {
						resource = rubber
						amount > 79
					}
					has_resources_amount = {
						resource = rubber
						amount < 124
					}
				}
				add_resource = {
					type = rubber
					amount = -10
						}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			}

						resource = rubber

				set_victory_points = {

					value = 5
				}
			}
			IF = {

					value = 5

					province = 10153
					value = 5
				}
			}
			IF = {

					var:ROOT.INS_stepping_stone_state = { state = 334 }
				}
				set_victory_points = {
					province = 10237
					value = 5
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 669 }
				limit = {
					is_fully_controlled_by = INS
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_state_category = small_island
							has_state_category = tiny_island
							has_state_category = enclave
						}
					}
					NOT = { region = 158 } #Not Java or Sumatra
					NOT = { region = 187 }
				}
				set_variable = { ROOT.INS_stepping_stone_state = THIS }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = INS_stepping_stone_state_flag

					}
				}
				add_core_of = INS
			}
			every_owned_state = {
